<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́кать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plákatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to complain <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, about someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cry, to weep

***пламенеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пламенеть.html>пламене́ть</a> (21986)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пла́мен-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plámen-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламенеть.html>пламене́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plamenétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to flame, to blaze</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to burn <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">with passion</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***пламень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пламень.html>пла́мень</a> (27543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Variant of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пла́мя</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plámja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пла́мен</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plámen</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">пла̏ме̄н</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">plámen</i> (gen. sg. <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">plaména</i>)), <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">plamen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">plameň</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">płomień</i>.
</p>

***пламя.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пла́мя</a> (2343)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">пламꙑ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plamy</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*polmy</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flame</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">по́лымя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólymja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">по́ломя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pólomja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, the inherited East Slavic forms.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пла́мя</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plámja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пла́мени</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пламена́</a></i>, <i>genitive plural</i> <span class="hypothetical-star">*</span><i class="Cyrl hypothetical" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пламя.html>пламён</a></i>)
</p>
<ol><li>flame</li>
<li>blaze</li></ol>

***план.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> (553)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">plan</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">planus</i>, possibly via <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">plan</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Plan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plan</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́на</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́нов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plan (set of intended actions), scheme</li>
<li>draft, plan, scheme, contrivance, road map</li>
<li>target, figure</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> marijuana</li></ol>

***планета.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́та</a> (1461)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">planéta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>planet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>больши́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:планета.html>плане́ты</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bolʹšíje <b>planéty</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">major planets</span></div></dd>

***планировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:планировать.html>планирова́ть</a> (5306)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планировать.html>плани́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">planírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спланировать.html>сплани́ровать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to plan, to project, to schedule
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:спланировать.html>сплани́ровать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">splanírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:запланировать.html>заплани́ровать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaplanírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to glide</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планировать.html>планирова́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">planirovátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">распланирова́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to level, to lay out</li></ol>

***планка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:планка.html>пла́нка</a> (12146)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">planca</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планка.html>пла́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планка.html>пла́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планка.html>пла́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:планка.html>пла́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plank, slat, lath</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a></li></ol>

***плановый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новый</a> (12353)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plan</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plánovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plan, planning
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:отдел.html>отде́л</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovyj</b> otdél</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>planning</b> department</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> target; systematic, planned
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйство.html>хозя́йство</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovoje</b> xozjájstvo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>planned</b> economy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:работа.html>рабо́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovaja</b> rabóta</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>planned</b> work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:задание.html>зада́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovoje</b> zadánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>target</b> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">figure</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>target</b> task</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:норма.html>но́рма</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расход.html>расхо́дов</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovaja</b> nórma rasxódov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">spending <b>target</b></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>target</b> standard of expenditure</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:цена.html>цена́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovaja</b> cená</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>target</b> price</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:капитальный.html>капита́льные</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вложение.html>вложе́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovyje</b> kapitálʹnyje vložénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>budgeted</b> capital expenditures</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>routine
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новый</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремонт.html>ремо́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovyj</b> remónt</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>scheduled</b> repair</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проверка.html>прове́рка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovaja</b> provérka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>routine</b> check/inspection</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:хирургический.html>хирурги́ческая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:операция.html>опера́ция</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovaja</b> xirurgíčeskaja operácija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>routine</b> surgery</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:плановый.html>пла́новое</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:технический.html>техни́ческое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обслуживание.html>обслу́живание</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plánovoje</b> texníčeskoje obslúživanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>routine</b> maintenance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

font-weight: bold;">Planchette</span></i>… instrument… est composé d'une petite planchette de… bois fortuni, longue amp; large d'un pied, si l'on veut, ou davantage amp; fort polie, amp; d'un genouïl qui lui est attaché en dessous au milieu. Ce genouil est composé d'une boule de cuivre, renfermée entre deux coquilles de même metal. La tigede ce genouil s'enboite autour d'un pied qu'on fiche dans la terre, lors qu'on se veut servir de l'instrument.</span> </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>

***пласт.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пласт.html>пласт</a> (8309)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">пластъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plastŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thin layer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*plastъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пласт.html>пласт</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plast</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пласт.html>пласта́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пласт.html>пласты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пласт.html>пласто́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>layer, sheet, stratum</li>
<li>bed <i>(a deposit of ore, coal etc.)</i></li></ol>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластик.html>пла́стика</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plástika</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластик.html>пла́стики</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластик.html>пла́стики</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластик.html>пла́стик</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>plastic art</li>

***пластический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пластический.html>пласти́ческий</a> (19835)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">plastique</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластический.html>пласти́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plastíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plastic art</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plastique</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plastic

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластичный.html>пласти́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plastíčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***пластичный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пластичный.html>пласти́чный</a> (32244)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">plast(ique)</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластичный.html>пласти́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plastíčnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пласти́чнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)пласти́чней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">physics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> biology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plastic</li>
<li>flexible or well-proportioned
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пластичный.html>пласти́чная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:балерина.html>балери́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plastíčnaja</b> balerína</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a flexible ballet dancer</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изящный.html>изя́щная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пластичный.html>пласти́чная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:скульптура.html>скульпту́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">izjáščnaja i <b>plastíčnaja</b> skulʹptúra</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a sculpture with compact and well-proportioned figures</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">plastic, plastical</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластический.html>пласти́ческий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">plastíčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пластмассовый.html>пластма́ссовый</a> (7350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластмасса.html>пластма́сса</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plastmássa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластмассовый.html>пластма́ссовый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plastmássovyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plastic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:пластмассовый.html>пластма́ссовая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бутылка.html>буты́лка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>plastmássovaja</b> butýlka</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>plastic</b> bottle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***пластырь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стырь</a> (14972)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стырь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">plastyrĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vulgar_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Vulgar Latin">Vulgar Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">*plastrum</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стырь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">plástyrʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стыря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стыри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стырей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> plaster, band-aid
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прикладывать.html>прикла́дывать</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стырь</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prikládyvatʹ <b>plástyrʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">put a plaster</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">naval</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> patch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подводить.html>подводи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:пластырь.html>пла́стырь</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">podvodítʹ <b>plástyrʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">secure a collision <a href = vnd.unilang:мат.html>mat</a></span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
